篇与健康生活有关的科普和故事，逐渐成长为国民级的新一代大众健康媒体。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">再过几天就是白露了，秋老虎的威力开始明显地日渐衰退。于是，不少人又开始折腾起「变白大计」。<br></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">虽说白不白，真一点不影响颜值和健康，但……变白了确实会更好买衣服、挑口红色号。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">而且，当你看着身边那些一同经历了夏季暴晒后，却依旧白得发光的小伙伴时，内心真抑制不住地羡慕嫉妒恨<img data-ratio=\"1\" data-type=\"png\" data-w=\"20\" style=\"display: inline-block; width: 28px; vertical-align: text-bottom; height: 28px; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/sz_mmbiz_png/Pvr3FasqXd5I9snUibu7FTUnl1ePaht3RI6qDbDTQwssTibUCmROOe2icR9Lrsjl2d4aSbIqL7G8ibEnLkDCKtjvgQ/640?wx_fmt=png\">！</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong>但其实，要想肌肤白皙无斑点，真没那么难。你只要——</strong></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;margin-bottom: 10px;text-align: center;\"><strong><span style=\"color: rgb(84, 84, 84);\">1. 做好防晒，不让黑素细胞工作</span></strong></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;margin-bottom: 10px;text-align: center;\"><strong><span style=\"color: rgb(84, 84, 84);\">2. 抑制、代谢黑色素</span></strong></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">因为紫外线的刺激，会让肌肤深处的黑素细胞产生黑色素。所以变白的第一步，就是要做好防晒，让黑素细胞接收不到生产指令，黑色素自然就会减少啦。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">不过，就算防晒做足，也难免会有漏网之鱼。这时，就需要你选择一些含有能抑制、代谢黑色素成分的护肤品，破坏、甚至消灭它。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong>考虑到前几天我们刚讲过并安利了不少的「防晒」好物，所以今儿个，我们就来给大家介绍 2 款能让你白皙无斑点的平价好物</strong>——</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p><p style=\"white-space: style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;text-align: right;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(160, 160, 160);font-size: 12px;\">— 广告 —</span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p></section><section style=\"margin-right: 0%;margin-bottom: 5px;margin-left: 0%;text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"margin-bottom: -6px;line-height: 1;padding-right: 5px;padding-left: 5px;font-size: 18px;letter-spacing: 0.4px;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong>1</strong></p></section><section style=\"width: 100%;height: 10px;background-color: rgba(116, 97, 255, 0.3);box-sizing: border-box;line-height: 0;\"><br></section></section></section><section style=\"margin-right: 0%;margin-bottom: 5px;margin-left: 0%;text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"margin-bottom: -6px;line-height: 1;padding-right: 5px;padding-left: 5px;font-size: 18px;letter-spacing: 0.4px;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong>添加 10% 黄金浓度原型 VC</strong></p></section><section style=\"width: 100%;height: 10px;background-color: rgba(116, 97, 255, 0.3);box-sizing: border-box;line-height: 0;\"><br></section></section></section><section style=\"margin-right: 0%;margin-bottom: 5px;margin-left: 0%;text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"margin-bottom: -6px;line-height: 1;padding-right: 5px;padding-left: 5px;font-size: 18px;letter-spacing: 0.4px;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong>有效直接抑制黑色素的美白精华</strong></p></section><section style=\"width: 100%;height: 10px;background-color: rgba(116, 97, 255, 0.3);box-sizing: border-box;line-height: 0;\"><br></section></section></section><section style=\"letter-spacing: 0.4px;padding-right: 10px;padding-left: 10px;color: rgb(84, 84, 84);box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p><p><img class=\"rich_pages\" data-backh=\"310\" data-backw=\"558\" data-ratio=\"0.5555555555555556\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"png\" data-w=\"1080\" style=\"width: 100%; height: auto; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/sz_mmbiz_png/Pvr3FasqXd5I9snUibu7FTUnl1ePaht3RVoLpZvKUIG00GsicbsTjx5ofMxl63yR0jpWZj5XfmibYibAT4vibY4E3pg/640?wx_fmt=png\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong>说到有效美白，那就不得不提经典的抗氧化美白成分——抗坏血酸，也就是我们俗称的维生素 C。</strong></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">为啥呢？</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">因为紫外线的照射，会让肌肤产生自由基。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">自由基会在肌肤里搞破坏，比如破坏蛋白质、破坏体内的酶、导致炎症和衰老……造成各种肌肤问题。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">所以，肌肤在感受到紫外线的刺激时，就会向黑素细胞发出指令——产生黑色素，抵抗紫外线。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong>而 VC 这个成分可以不需要「劳烦」黑色素细胞动手，就消灭自由基。</strong>这样，就能在一定程度上抑制黑色素的生成，减少黑色素，自然就不会变黑啦。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong>如果黑色素已经被分泌出来了，VC 还能趁它处于不稳定状态时，干扰它继续生成。</strong></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong><br></strong></p><p style=\"text-align: center;\"><img class=\"rich_pages\" data-backh=\"372\" data-backw=\"558\" data-ratio=\"0.66640625\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1280\" style=\"width: 100%; height: auto; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/sz_mmbiz_jpg/Pvr3FasqXd5I9snUibu7FTUnl1ePaht3RjP18lEMaIwQGOuHxl60qrjV5fYIIRJpyYEIJkeED4OH5jD1dGIfdicg/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></p><p style=\"text-align: center;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(160, 160, 160);font-size: 12px;\">图片来源：图虫</span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">不过，遗憾的是 VC 虽好却不够稳定，所以<strong>市面上大多数的精华，会选择使用间接成分——维生素 C 衍生物。</strong>通过它在肌肤内部转化为 VC，起到消灭自由基，让肌肤恢复白净的作用。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">可这样的间接转化，很大程度上会削减 VC 的效果。好在<strong>怡婷美这款美白精华，采用的是原型维生素 C，不需要转化，就能直接有效地对肌肤产生作用。</strong></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong>更重要的是，它的 VC 添加量高达 10%。</strong>这样的黄金浓度，既不会浓度太低隔靴搔痒，又不会浓度太高，刺激肌肤造成肌肤敏感。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p><p style=\"text-align: center;\"><img class=\"rich_pages js_insertlocalimg\" data-backh=\"372\" data-backw=\"558\" data-ratio=\"0.66640625\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1280\" style=\"width: 100%; height: auto; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/sz_mmbiz_jpg/Pvr3FasqXd5I9snUibu7FTUnl1ePaht3RMicCStOWWibrqQSCMkuPQPhQTf86yeTJcPpHVhRibMGKMP62cRUYibNb5w/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">而且，除了 VC ，它还添加了维生素 E<span style=\"color: rgb(160, 160, 160);\">（生育酚乙酸酯）</span>。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">要知道这两，那可是护肤品的经典老组合了。搭配在一起，抗氧化的效果简直是 1+1&gt;2。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong>再配上能让肌肤更加紧致的咖啡因、能舒缓肌肤的甘草酸二甲、以及⻆鲨烷、丁二醇等多种经典保湿剂</strong>，既能有效消灭自由基，抑制黑色素生成，又能滋养呵护肌肤，让肌肤软软嫩嫩。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"text-align: center;\"><img class=\"rich_pages\" data-backh=\"372\" data-backw=\"558\" data-ratio=\"0.6666666666666666\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1080\" style=\"width: 100%; height: auto; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/sz_mmbiz_jpg/Pvr3FasqXd5I9snUibu7FTUnl1ePaht3RfKUd726P0iabD53YDDkjG29WVPmMNIQS4CFBWWWARVqsSibOUJpicRGwQ/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">考虑的原型 VC 的不稳定性，它特意采用遮光瓶身 + 长管按压头的设计，避免光照，减少空气接触，确保 VC 的活性。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">按出来是黄色的膏状，类似黄油的质地，有股淡淡的橙子味。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">比起一般精华略显厚重，但一点不油腻，也很容易推开，非常好吸收。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">吸收完，肌肤会展现一种哑光的丝绒质地。就连摸起来的肤感，似乎也光滑了不少。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">不仅可以全脸美白，还可以局部涂抹在脸上因为长痘等原因色素沉积，导致肤色不均匀的地方。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"text-align: center;\"><img border-box;\">而快节奏的都市生活，使得加班、熬夜成为生活的常态。再加上眼周肌肤比面部薄很多，又分布着大量的神经纤维和毛细血管，<strong>一旦熬夜或者用眼过度，眼部血管中的去氧血红蛋白会增多，眼睑处的肌肤就容易显露出青紫色——产生「血管型黑眼圈」。</strong></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p><p style=\"text-align: center;\"><img class=\"rich_pages\" data-backh=\"310\" data-backw=\"558\" data-ratio=\"0.5554830287206266\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"png\" style=\"font-size: 16px;box-sizing: border-box;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(160, 160, 160);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">2019 年 11 月 29 号那天，是一个周五，黄杰像往常一样来到医院上班。他是湖北省武汉大学人民医院胸外科的主任。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">早晨交班的时候，值班医生告诉他，凌晨来了一个患者，情况比较严重，今天需要尽快处理。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">与此同时，重症医学科的主任魏捷也给他打来电话，通知他参加会诊，最好在 24 小时内手术。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">两人说的是同一个患者。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">黄杰没想到的是，这场聚集了 10 个科室、30 多位医生、耗时一整天的「生死急救」，竟始于患者一个小小的疏忽。</p></section></section></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" border-box;\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">吃鱼，卡住了</strong></p></section><section style=\"width: 100%;height: 10px;background-color: rgb(239, 241, 236);box-sizing: border-box;line-height: 0;\"><br></section></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br inline-block;width: 92%;vertical-align: top;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"text-align: justify;color: rgb(84, 84, 84);line-height: 1.8;letter-spacing: 0.4px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">患者老林是半夜在儿子的陪同下来到急诊的。来这里之前，他已经跑了好多家医院。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">老林今年 50 多岁，湖北咸宁人。两天前，家里吃了一次鱼，他不小心吞下一根鱼刺，卡在了喉咙里。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">卡住后，他也没放在心上，只是按照土办法，吞了两口饭。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">当时，他并没有感觉到什么不舒服，也就没当回事，还以为这根鱼刺已经像之前一样，随着饭团咽下去了。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">28 号这天，他突然感觉到剧烈胸痛，于是赶忙到咸宁当地的医院检查。医生很快安排了 CTA（CT 血管造影）。<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">结果发现，一根鱼刺样的异物卡在了老林的食道内，并且已经刺穿了食道壁，扎进了胸主动脉。</strong></p></section></section></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;justify-content: center;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 92%;vertical-align: top;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"text-align: justify;color: rgb(84, 84, 84);line-height: 1.8;letter-spacing: 0.4px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">胸主动脉是人体最粗大的动脉血管，血管压力很高，一旦形成破口，就会引发大出血，直接危及生命，甚至根本没有抢救的机会。</p></section></section></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 92%;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"1.1731481\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1080\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; max-width: 600px\" 版</p></section></section></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: justify;color: rgb(84, 84, 84);line-height: 1.8;letter-spacing: 0.4px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">病情棘手，当地的医院不敢接收，建议老林赶紧到武汉治疗。因为情况过于凶险，武汉的几家医院也觉得难度过大，无法处理。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">几经辗转，29 号凌晨，他来到了武汉大学人民医院。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">第二天一大早，重症医学科的魏捷听值班医生报告了这个病例。她看到检查结果后，发现鱼刺像一把「弯刀」架在食道和主动脉之间，就像主动脉上突兀地长出了一根刺。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">这根鱼刺就是老林体内的一颗定时炸弹，随时有可能发生「爆炸」，导致大出血，后果不堪设想。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">老林必须尽快进行手术，取出鱼刺，防止情况进一步恶化。但如果盲目拔出鱼刺，很容易形成主动脉破口。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">这就需要多个科室的专家协商确定手术方案。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">慎重起见，魏捷将老林转入重症医学科，对他实施浅镇静，密切监护。同时，她第一时间呼叫了全院大会诊。</p></section></section></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;justify-content: auto;align-self: center;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: border-box;\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">鱼刺不见了？</strong></p></section><section style=\"width: 100%;height: 10px;background-color: rgb(239, 241, 236);box-sizing: border-box;line-height: 0;\"><br></section></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;justify-content: center;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 92%;vertical-align: top;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"text-align: justify;color: rgb(84, 84, 84);line-height: 1.8;letter-spacing: 0.4px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">胸外科、心血管外科、耳鼻喉-头颈外科、消化内科、放射科、麻醉科……</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">10 个科室的 30 多位医生紧急聚集在一起，开启了一场「主动脉营救战」。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">专家团讨论经过详细讨论，确定了微创取刺的手术方案：先由心血管外科的医生为老林植入一个主动脉覆膜支架，堵住因鱼刺造成的血管缺口，再由消化内科的医生尝试利用胃镜取刺。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">手术前，老林在广东打工的爱人也赶到武汉，完成了术前谈话和签字。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">29 日下午，老林被推入导管室。实施麻醉后，心血管外科的医生将主动脉支架植入老林的体内，堵住已经糜烂的血管缺口。</p></section></section></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: 14px;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);letter-spacing: 0.6px;padding-right: 10px;padding-left: 10px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">主动脉支架</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">▼</p></section></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 92%;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"1.0777778\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1080\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/sz_mmbiz_jpg/Pvr3FasqXd5I9snUibu7FTUnl1ePaht3REmX0ic9iaQicWDPe3TlvPgua3cKjTst1lsLqakbcjMeStiarPnkqqibN7Xg/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></section></section><section style=\"margin-top: 15px;margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"text-align: center;font-size: 12px;color: rgb(206, 206, 206);line-height: 1.8;letter-spacing: 0.6px;padding-right: 10px;padding-left: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">图片来源：武汉大学人民医院</p></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"color: rgb(79, 79, 79);line-height: 1.8;letter-spacing: 0.4px;padding-right: 10px;padding-left: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">放置支架后，老林紧接着进入了手术室。消化内科的医生开始通过胃镜确认鱼刺位置，准备取出。就在这时，意外发生了——<br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">术前已经精准定位在在食道与主动脉间的鱼刺，现在却不见了。</strong></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">在胃镜中，医生们只看到食道中下段的地方有一个糜烂面，但鱼刺却不见踪影。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">他们怀疑，鱼刺可能已经随着一些动作自然脱落，进入了胃里，于是就先对食道进行了修补，准备把老林送回重症监护室继续观察。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">一切基本完成时，有医生觉得不放心，给黄杰打了电话询问。了解具体情况后，作为胸外科主任，黄杰给出了判断——鱼刺不会被吞到胃里。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">随着食道的蠕动，或者主动脉内血流的强劲冲击，鱼刺有很大概率会穿出食道，进入纵膈或者主动脉。</strong></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">无论是哪种情况，都必须迅速把它找出来。如果鱼刺留在体内，一定会造成严重感染，甚至刺破主动脉，引发大出血，后果不堪设想。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">而此时已经没有了微创取刺的可能，必须尽快开胸探查。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">手术方案立即调整，黄杰接力上了手术台。</p></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin-right: border-box;\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">开胸</strong></p></section><section style=\"width: 100%;height: 10px;background-color: rgb(239, 241, 236);box-sizing: border-box;line-height: 0;\"><br></section></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;justify-content: center;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 92%;vertical-align: top;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"text-align: justify;color: rgb(84, 84, 84);line-height: 1.8;letter-spacing: 0.4px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">事实证明，黄杰的判断是正确的。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">开胸之后，他先小心翼翼地松解胸腔的黏连，把食道和主动脉分开，然后清理干净分泌物和出血。视野渐渐清晰，他发现，主动脉外有一个 3 毫米左右的小尖刺。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">他用血管钳夹住小尖刺，一点点往外拔，竟拔出了一根 4 厘米长的鱼刺——鱼刺果然是穿出了食道，几乎全部扎进主动脉内。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">顺利取出鱼刺后，黄杰又立即对食道和主动脉进行了修补，然后重新固定胸骨、缝合。</p></section></section></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"margin-right: 0%;margin-bottom: 10px;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"text-align: center;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);letter-spacing: 0.6px;padding-right: 10px;padding-left: 10px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">取出的鱼刺</p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">▼</p></section></section><section style=\"text-align: 1.8;letter-spacing: 0.6px;padding-right: 10px;padding-left: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">图片来源：武汉大学人民医院</p></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;justify-content: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"text-align: justify;color: rgb(84, 84, 84);line-height: 1.8;letter-spacing: 0.4px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">手术结束已经是晚上九点。老林回到了 ICU（重症监护室），在那里住了 3 天。情况稳定后，他转入普通病房，在医院住了一周，顺利出院。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">一个月后，老林再次去武汉复查。因为发现及时，处理得当，他的感染并不严重，恢复得很好。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">他还给黄杰带去了一块匾额，感谢他的「妙手回春」。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">黄杰说，在他的从医生涯里，这样的事情并不少见，几乎每年都会有一二十例。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">就在前年，他曾遇到一个患者，也是鱼刺穿入了主动脉，正准备处理的时候，突然发生大出血，还没来得及抢救，就去世了。</p></section></section></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">鱼刺卡喉，应该怎么办？</strong></p></section><section style=\"width: 100%;height: 10px;background-color: rgb(239, 241, 236);box-sizing: border-box;line-height: 0;\"><br></section></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;justify-content: center;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 92%;vertical-align: top;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"text-align: justify;color: rgb(84, 84, 84);line-height: 1.8;letter-spacing: 0.4px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">日常饮食中，鱼刺卡喉并不少见，但如果处理不当，有可能造成严重的后果。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><ul class=\"list-paddingleft-2\"><li style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;margin-bottom: 10px;\">首先，喝醋并不能软化鱼刺，反而可能刺激甚至灼伤已经受损的食道黏膜。</section></li><li style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">其次，像老林一样 ，用饭团、馒头把鱼刺吞进去，也是非常危险的。因为这样很可能把位置较浅的刺推得更深，更难取出。</p></li></ul><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">你以为卡在喉咙里的鱼刺会这样：</p></section></section></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin-right: 0%;margin-left: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">但事实很可能是这样：</p></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"margin-right: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">甚至这样：</p></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 92%;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"0.5633333\" data-type=\"gif\" data-w=\"300\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/sz_mmbiz_gif/Pvr3FasqXd5I9snUibu7FTUnl1ePaht3RVAVleuzHBvnABJmvGKaDVVLOYTlgUNh81I1UttZmhOGxIibEKkaXs9Q/640?wx_fmt=gif\"></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;justify-content: center;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 92%;vertical-align: top;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"text-align: justify;color: rgb(84, 84, 84);line-height: 1.8;letter-spacing: 0.4px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">如果鱼刺比较粗大或者比较硬，很有可能刺破食道，造成食道穿孔、纵膈感染，或者像老林的情况一样，直接插入主动脉，随时可能导致大出血，危及生命。</p></section></section></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 92%;vertical-align: top;background-color: rgb(246, 246, 246);height: auto;border-width: 1px;border-radius: 0px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgb(239, 241, 236);box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"margin: 20px 0% 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"margin-bottom: -6px;line-height: 1;padding-right: 5px;padding-left: 5px;font-size: 18px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">正确的处理方法</strong></p></section><section style=\"width: 100%;height: 10px;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box;line-height: 0;\"><br></section></section></section><section style=\"margin: 15px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"text-align: justify;color: rgb(84, 84, 84);line-height: 1.8;padding-right: 15px;padding-left: 15px;letter-spacing: 0.4px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><ul class=\"list-paddingleft-2\"><li style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;margin-bottom: 10px;\">如果鱼刺卡得比较浅，张嘴就能看到，可以找人帮忙，小心地用镊子夹出。</section></li><li style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;margin-bottom: 10px;\">也可以试着用力咳嗽，很多时候，细小的鱼刺会跟着气流脱落下来。</section></li><li style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 0.4px;box-sizing: border-box;\">如果鱼刺卡得比较深，刺痛感剧烈，就要尽快去医院，交给专业医生处理。</span><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></li></ul></section></section></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;justify-content: center;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 92%;vertical-align: top;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"text-align: justify;color: rgb(84, 84, 84);line-height: 1.8;letter-spacing: 0.4px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">其实，自然卡住的鱼刺一般都不会太深。如果第一时间去医院，不需要花很多钱，耳鼻喉科的医生很快就能搞定。<br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">如果使用了「土方法」自行处理，反而可能因为吞咽等外力加剧病情，就需要动用喉镜、消化内镜甚至开胸手术了。不仅费钱费力，人还跟着受罪。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">马上就是中秋了，阖家团圆，家人聚餐的时候，一定要小心。<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">吃鱼时，要认真剔除鱼刺，细嚼慢咽，不要分神，老人和孩子尤其要注意。</strong></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">也可以直接选用鱼刺较少的鱼，比如龙利鱼、三文鱼、鳕鱼等。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">除了鱼刺之外，锐利的鸡骨头和枣核也是常见的食道异物。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">如果发生了异物卡喉的情况，千万不要抱有侥幸心理，记得正确处理，及时就医。</strong></p></section></section></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"text-align: justify;color: rgb(84, 84, 84);letter-spacing: 0.4px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">这主要是来自于一个流言：</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p></section><section style=\"justify-content: center;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 92%;vertical-align: top;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;padding-top: 3px;padding-bottom: 6px;border-width: 1px;border-radius: 0px;border-style: solid none;border-color: rgb(239, 241, 236) rgb(219, 219, 219);width: 100%;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"text-align: left;margin: -20px 0% -5px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 30px;height: 35px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);padding-right: 5px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"0.6437768\" data-type=\"svg\" data-w=\"233\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; height: auto !important; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_svg/uI5pczeERTaojrtwdASJEM7iaAZJrrxThoWRp0iaVNviaLyVOsMQBAK2fic6sHZSDZeIXBu9IGUrDcETDxWx2MIJNWLGDDRdRh6Y/640?wx_fmt=svg\"></section></section></section></section><section style=\"text-align: justify;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"padding-right: 5px;padding-left: 5px;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);line-height: 1.8;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"text-align: justify;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">味精（谷氨酸钠）加热到 120℃ 以上时，可能产生焦谷氨酸钠。而这种物质不仅有毒，还是「致癌」的罪魁祸首。</p></section></section><section style=\"text-align: justify;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"text-align: right;margin-right: 0%;margin-bottom: -30px;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 30px;height: 35px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);padding-left: 5px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"0.6437768\" data-type=\"svg\" data-w=\"233\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; height: auto !important; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_svg/uI5pczeERTaojrtwdASJEM7iaAZJrrxThkkxEG1Z2eXW1Il39icwoYseHYwEtCjpcwBCtTICxmGATib4f53RU8W7eKC4icV0vqCO/640?wx_fmt=svg\"></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section style=\"text-align: justify;color: rgb(84, 84, 84);letter-spacing: 0.4px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">这个说法的前半句的确没错：谷氨酸钠加热到 120℃ 以上时确实会产生焦谷氨酸钠。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">但焦谷氨酸钠对人体是安全的，不仅毒性极低，而且并不会「致癌」。</strong></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">FDA 将味精划入公认安全（Generally Recognized as Safe）的产品/成分。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"justify-content: center;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;border-width: 0px;border-radius: 0px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"0.677193\" data-type=\"png\" data-w=\"570\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; height: auto !important; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/sz_mmbiz_png/Pvr3FasqXd5I9snUibu7FTUnl1ePaht3RsKTx7a8ShmeicjtkNAhQVPiaiax1vqBRTb6a8dXqGKUmVWOYHocwiagVew/640?wx_fmt=png\"></section></section></section></section><section style=\"margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/sz_mmbiz_png/Pvr3FasqXd5I9snUibu7FTUnl1ePaht3RZ75ZsnKIfLCicqoI85iaZCdLbaIicFTpu98w6YY864UCiaD0NQA6N3w1Sg/640?wx_fmt=png\"></section></section><section style=\"margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;background-color: rgb(246, 246, 246);padding: 10px;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"margin: 5px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"font-size: 14px;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);text-align: justify;line-height: 1.8;padding-right: 5px;padding-left: 5px;letter-spacing: 0.4px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">也因为对于味精的争议较大，FDA 针对味精的相关疑问做了全面的解读。</p></section></section></section></section><section style=\"text-align: justify;color: rgb(84, 84, 84);letter-spacing: 0.4px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 0.4px;box-sizing: border-box;\">而焦谷氨酸钠在很多日常生活领域都有应用，比如说化妆品、药品等。它被</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 0.4px;box-sizing: border-box;\">添加在化妆品中可以起到乳化和保湿的作用，怎么就致癌了呢？</span><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"letter-spacing: 0.4px;box-sizing: border-box;\">我们一般建议快出锅时再添加味精，不是因为加热致癌，而是高温让味精变成了焦谷氨酸钠，失去了鲜味。</strong><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">谷氨酸钠真的挺安全的。</p></section><section style=\"text-align: justify;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"text-align: justify;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"border-bottom: 2px solid rgb(246, 71, 67);display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;padding-left: 5px;padding-right: 5px;margin-bottom: -1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);line-height: 2;font-size: 17px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">吃味精会缺锌？</strong></p></section><section style=\"border-bottom: 1px solid rgba(0, 0, 0, 0);width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;line-height: 0;\"><section style=\"line-height: 0;width: 0px;\"><svg viewbox=\"0 0 1 1\" style=\"vertical-align:top;\"></svg></section></section></section></section><section style=\"text-align: justify;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"text-align: justify;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"text-align: justify;color: rgb(84, 84, 84);letter-spacing: 0.4px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">关于味精的争议还瞄向了孩子，媒体上的一些报道提到：</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"justify-content: center;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 92%;vertical-align: top;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;padding-top: 3px;padding-bottom: 6px;border-width: 1px;border-radius: 0px;border-style: solid none;border-color: rgb(239, 241, 236) rgb(219, 219, 219);width: 100%;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"text-align: left;margin: -20px 0% -5px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 30px;height: 35px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);padding-right: 5px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"0.6437768\" data-type=\"svg\" data-w=\"233\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; height: auto !important; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_svg/uI5pczeERTaojrtwdASJEM7iaAZJrrxThoWRp0iaVNviaLyVOsMQBAK2fic6sHZSDZeIXBu9IGUrDcETDxWx2MIJNWLGDDRdRh6Y/640?wx_fmt=svg\"></section></section></section></section><section style=\"text-align: justify;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"padding-right: 5px;padding-left: 5px;text-align: justify;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);line-height: 1.8;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">吃过多的味精会缺锌。味精中含有的谷氨酸钠在被人体吸收之后，会与血液中的锌化合，转化为谷氨酸锌，直接排出体外。</p></section></section><section style=\"text-align: justify;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"text-align: right;margin-right: 0%;margin-bottom: -30px;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 30px;height: 35px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);padding-left: 5px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"0.6437768\" data-type=\"svg\" data-w=\"233\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; height: auto !important; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_svg/uI5pczeERTaojrtwdASJEM7iaAZJrrxThkkxEG1Z2eXW1Il39icwoYseHYwEtCjpcwBCtTICxmGATib4f53RU8W7eKC4icV0vqCO/640?wx_fmt=svg\"></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section style=\"text-align: justify;color: rgb(84, 84, 84);letter-spacing: 0.4px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">然而，当我们检索信源和资料之后发现，没有任何「谷氨酸钠导致锌缺乏」的研究。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">网上关于「味精吃多了缺锌」的说法，大多来自没有根据的文章。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">此外，流言中「谷氨酸锌」这种物质，我们检索后还发现一个有趣事实：</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">谷氨酸锌本身就是研发出来当做锌的补充剂使用的。</strong></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">有一些证据证明，谷氨酸锌的生物可利用性比起目前市场上最常见的葡萄糖酸锌来的还要高。这和流言正好相反。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">也就是说，谷氨酸锌不仅不会导致「缺锌」，而且还可能是一个很好的「补锌」材料。</strong></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">真的造谣一张嘴，辟谣跑断腿。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">除了这些争议，还有人觉得味精看起来像化工合成的，不是天然的而不吃。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"justify-content: center;box-sizing: border-box;\" border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">这可真想多了！</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">让食物变得有鲜味的成分谷氨酸<span style=\"font-size: 14px;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);\">（人感受到味精的鲜味主要是因为其中游离的谷氨酸）</span>，这种成分其实你每天都会吃到，它存在于大量的天然食物中，根本不用担心。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p></section><section style=\"min-height: 40px;margin: 10px border-box;\"><br></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">味精的核心工艺是「发酵」的过程，而不是大家想象中的「人工合成」。<span style=\"letter-spacing: 0.4px;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif>现在发酵的原料比较多用到的是大家更为熟悉的淀粉或者糖蜜。</span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif>发酵法造价便宜，产量大，也</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 0.4px;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans top;border-left: 2px dashed rgb(160, 160, 160);border-bottom-left-radius: 0px;padding-left: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">一位叫 Robert Ho Man Kwok 的人来信，自称来美国已经好几年了，经常去中餐馆，每次去中餐馆用餐后都会出现一些奇怪的症状，比如脖颈后麻木，心悸，疲劳等。他怀疑这是由于中餐馆在菜肴中添加了味精所致。</p></section></section></section></section></section><section style=\"text-align: justify;color: rgb(84, 84, 84);letter-spacing: 0.4px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">随后，欧美群众发起了「抵制味精」的运动，而各个中餐馆只好打出了「不添加味精」的招牌，才能重新获得顾客。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">也正因为这些报道和猜测，学术界开始认真研究味精，多年的研究却发现结论恰恰相反。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;text-align: left;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"width: 0px;margin-bottom: -10px;transform: rotate(0deg);-webkit-transform: rotate(0deg);-moz-transform: rotate(0deg);-o-transform: rotate(0deg);border-top: 5px solid rgb(255, 255, 255);border-left: 5px solid rgb(255, 255, 255);border-right: 5px solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 5px solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;line-height: 0;\"><section style=\"line-height: 0;width: 0px;\"><svg viewbox=\"0 0 1 1\" style=\"vertical-align:top;\"></svg></section></section><section style=\"background-color: rgb(18, 37, 52);padding: 3px 10px;text-align: center;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(246, 246, 246);box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">2000 年，「中餐馆综合征」无法复现</strong></p></section><section style=\"width: 0px;margin-top: -10px;margin-left: auto;transform: rotate(0deg);-webkit-transform: rotate(0deg);-moz-transform: rotate(0deg);-o-transform: rotate(0deg);border-right: 5px solid rgb(255, 255, 255);border-bottom: 5px solid rgb(255, 255, 255);border-top: 5px solid transparent !important;border-left: 5px solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;line-height: 0;\"><section style=\"line-height: 0;width: 0px;\"><svg viewbox=\"0 0 1 1\" style=\"vertical-align:top;\"></svg></section></section></section></section><section style=\"margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;padding-left: 16px;border-width: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;border-left: 2px dashed rgb(160, 160, 160);border-bottom-left-radius: 0px;padding-left: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">研究对自称吃味精会出现不适症状的人群做了研究，结果发现这些人的症状很难再复现。大剂量的单一摄入味精才可能有少量不良反应出现，但如果与食物一起吃则不会有这样的反应。</p></section></section></section></section></section><section style=\"text-align: justify;color: rgb(84, 84, 84);letter-spacing: 0.4px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p><p style=\"letter-spacing: 0.4px;text-size-adjust: 100%;\"><br></p><span style=\"letter-spacing: 0.4px;text-size-adjust: 100%;\">还有研究者认为头晕、不适可能纯粹是心理因素导致的。</span></section><section style=\"text-align: justify;color: rgb(84, 84, 84);letter-spacing: 0.4px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">而现在很多人觉得吃完餐馆的菜感觉到的口干舌燥，很大程度上可能也和「钠」摄入过多有关。</strong></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></strong></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">通常，1 克味精（谷氨酸钠）中含有的钠 136 毫克，而 1 克的盐则有钠 393 毫克，也就是 1 克盐的钠含量相当于 3 克味精里有的，味精的钠少多了。<strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></strong></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p></section><section style=\"margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"0.561\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1000\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; box-sizing: border-box; height: auto !important; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/sz_mmbiz_jpg/Pvr3FasqXd5I9snUibu7FTUnl1ePaht3RJgeVibhnJ4Rdpv1QZ6B7cESoeeqwmDiabArA9nQ4KwCgdRn9fqWFEdlQ/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></section></section><section style=\"text-align: justify;color: rgb(84, 84, 84);letter-spacing: 0.4px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"text-align: center;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 12px;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;\">图片来源：站酷海洛</span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 0.4px;box-sizing: border-box;\">「钠」不仅存在于味精中，还更多存在于盐及其他的调味品里。</span><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;text-align: left;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"width: 0px;margin-bottom: -10px;transform: rotate(0deg);-webkit-transform: rotate(0deg);-moz-transform: rotate(0deg);-o-transform: rotate(0deg);border-top: 5px solid rgb(255, 255, 255);border-left: 5px solid rgb(255, 255, 255);border-right: 5px solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 5px solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;line-height: 0;\"><section style=\"line-height: 0;width: 0px;\"><svg viewbox=\"0 0 1 1\" style=\"vertical-align:top;\"></svg></section></section><section style=\"background-color: rgb(18, 37, 52);padding: 3px 10px;text-align: center;color: rgb(246, 246, 246);box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">2019 年，成都 10 家餐馆菜品钠含量评估</strong></span></p></section><section style=\"width: 0px;margin-top: -10px;margin-left: auto;transform: rotate(0deg);-webkit-transform: rotate(0deg);-moz-transform: rotate(0deg);-o-transform: rotate(0deg);border-right: 5px solid rgb(255, 255, 255);border-bottom: 5px solid rgb(255, 255, 255);border-top: 5px solid transparent !important;border-left: 5px solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;line-height: 0;\"><section style=\"line-height: 0;width: 0px;\"><svg viewbox=\"0 0 1 1\" style=\"vertical-align:top;\"></svg></section></section></section></section><section style=\"margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;padding-left: 16px;border-width: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;border-left: 2px dashed rgb(160, 160, 160);border-bottom-left-radius: 0px;padding-left: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">此项调查发现 84% 的菜钠含量超过 800 毫克（相当于 2 克盐），最高的凉菜每 100 克就有近 1000 毫克的钠，达到每日推荐量的一半。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">而其中的钠 40% 来自盐，20% 来自味精/鸡精，20% 来自其他调味品。</p></section></section></section></section></section><section style=\"text-align: justify;color: rgb(84, 84, 84);letter-spacing: 0.4px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">也就是说，餐馆中味精对于「钠」的贡献并不大。提醒厨师少放味精倒不如少放盐来得重要。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">在感官科学中，鲜味和咸味的刺激有「协同增效」的效果。假设同样是加 1 克盐加 1 克味精会比加 2 克的盐更咸一些。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">所以，如果饭菜中最后准备添加一些味精来提鲜，那么，在一开始制作的时候，盐就可以少加一些，甚至不加，最后也能实现同样的美味。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">这样说来，味精又安全又让食物更美味，还便宜，这么优秀，就没啥缺点吗？</p></section><section style=\"text-align: justify;color: rgb(84, 84, 84);letter-spacing: 0.4px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p></section><section style=\"margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"border-bottom: 2px solid rgb(246, 71, 67);display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;padding-left: 5px;padding-right: 5px;margin-bottom: -1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);line-height: 2;font-size: 17px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></strong></p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">使用味精同样要控制量</strong></p></section><section style=\"border-bottom: 1px solid rgba(0, 0, 0, 0);width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;line-height: 0;\"><section style=\"line-height: 0;width: 0px;\"><svg viewbox=\"0 0 1 1\" style=\"vertical-align:top;\"></svg></section></section></section></section><section style=\"text-align: justify;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"text-align: justify;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"text-align: justify;color: rgb(84, 84, 84);letter-spacing: 0.4px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 0.4px;box-sizing: border-box;\">味精本质还是一种钠盐，虽然同等重量下，味精比盐少三分之二的钠，但如果加太多，也有钠摄入过量的风险。</span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">目前中国人普遍钠摄入过量，所以用味精和用盐一样，还是要控制量。</strong></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">另外，需要注意的是，千万不要在加足量盐之后，再去额外添加味精。这样做反而会增加钠的摄入量。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">平时用味精适量加就好，要是真的为了鲜味，大把大把加，那也是非常不建议的。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">也许还是会有不少人会说，虽然味精没啥问题，但也依然不会选择用味精。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">遗憾的是，不买味精，不代表没有吃到味精。日常生活中的调味品，根本没有离开过味精。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"border-bottom: 2px solid rgb(246, 71, 67);display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;padding-left: 5px;padding-right: 5px;margin-bottom: -1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);line-height: 2;font-size: 17px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">日常调味品离不开味精</strong></p></section><section style=\"border-bottom: 1px solid rgba(0, 0, 0, 0);width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;line-height: 0;\"><section style=\"line-height: 0;width: 0px;\"><svg viewbox=\"0 0 1 1\" style=\"vertical-align:top;\"></svg></section></section></section></section><section style=\"text-align: justify;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"text-align: justify;color: rgb(84, 84, 84);letter-spacing: 0.4px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">拿市面上现在很多人选择的鸡精来看，本质还是味精，它的配料表第一位就是「味精」。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"justify-content: center;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"margin-right: border-box;\">鸡精里会添加一些其他的鲜味成分（比如呈味核苷酸二钠等），让调味料的鲜味更丰富一些。两者的价格也相差 2 倍以上。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"text-align: border-box;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 0.4px;box-sizing: border-box;\">只要在配料表中出现了「谷氨酸钠」或者「味精」字样，那这个产品其实就已经添加了味精。</span><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">甚至在一些和鲜味完全无关的调味料中，也会添加味精（谷氨酸钠），比如蚝油、料酒，甚至是醋里面可能都有。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p></section><section style=\"margin: 10px 0% 5px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"font-size: 12px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing:
